across multiple interconnected packages in kubernetes/kubernetes:\\n\\n## Core Authorization Engine\\n\\nThe primary RBAC authorization logic is located in plugin/pkg/auth/authorizer/rbac/rbac.go. The RBACAuthorizer struct implements the authorizer.Authorizer interface and contains an Authorize method that evaluates authorization requests. The Authorize method uses a RequestToRuleMapper interface to resolve policy rules for a given user. The authorization flow uses an authorizingVisitor pattern that short-circuits on first match, checking each applicable rule using the RuleAllows function which matches verbs, API groups, resources, and resource names against the request attributes.\\n\\n## Subject Access Evaluator\\n\\nThe SubjectAccessEvaluator is defined in plugin/pkg/auth/authorizer/rbac/subject_locator.go and implements the SubjectLocator interface. It resolves all subjects that can perform a specific action using the RoleToRuleMapper interface to determine which roles are applicable to different users and groups.\\n\\n## Policy Rule Resolution - DefaultRuleResolver\\n\\nThe pkg/registry/rbac/validation/rule.go file contains the DefaultRuleResolver, which implements the AuthorizationRuleResolver interface and is responsible for resolving PolicyRules for users. Key methods include:\\n- RulesFor: Returns all applicable rules for a user in a namespace\\n- VisitRulesFor: Iterates through all applicable rules using a visitor pattern\\n- GetRoleReferenceRules: Resolves rules referenced by RoleBinding or ClusterRoleBinding objects\\n\\nThe DefaultRuleResolver works by examining ClusterRoleBindings and RoleBindings to find those that apply to the user (based on user name, group membership, or service account), then retrieving the actual PolicyRules from the referenced Role or ClusterRole objects.\\n\\n## SubjectAccessReview REST Handlers\\n\\nFour REST handlers are implemented for different SubjectAccessReview APIs:\\n1. pkg/registry/authorization/subjectaccessreview/rest.go - Cluster-wide SubjectAccessReview\\n2. pkg/registry/authorization/localsubjectaccessreview/rest.go - Namespace-scoped LocalSubjectAccessReview\\n3. pkg/registry/authorization/selfsubjectaccessreview/rest.go - Self-check SelfSubjectAccessReview\\n4. pkg/registry/authorization/selfsubjectrulesreview/rest.go - Rule enumeration SelfSubjectRulesReview\\n\\nThese REST handlers are registered via the RESTStorageProvider in pkg/registry/authorization/rest/storage_authorization.go.\\n\\n## Bootstrap RBAC Policies\\n\\nDefault RBAC policies are defined in plugin/pkg/auth/authorizer/rbac/bootstrappolicy/:\\n- policy.go: Main bootstrap policies defining default roles and bindings\\n- controller_policy.go: Policies for built-in controllers\\n- namespace_policy.go: Namespace-scoped default roles\\n\\n## Escalation Prevention\\n\\nThe system prevents privilege escalation through several mechanisms:\\n\\n1. pkg/registry/rbac/escalation_check.go contains:\\n   - EscalationAllowed: Checks if user is in the system:masters group\\n   - RoleEscalationAuthorized: Checks if user is explicitly authorized to escalate role permissions\\n   - BindingAuthorized: Checks if user is authorized to bind a specific role\\n\\n2. Policy-based storage implementations enforce escalation checks:\\n   - pkg/registry/rbac/role/policybased/storage.go\\n   - pkg/registry/rbac/clusterrole/policybased/storage.go\\n   - pkg/registry/rbac/rolebinding/policybased/storage.go\\n   - pkg/registry/rbac/clusterrolebinding/policybased/storage.go\\n\\n3. Escalation validation via pkg/registry/rbac/validation/:\\n   - rule.go: ConfirmNoEscalation function ensures users cannot grant permissions they don't have\\n   - internal_version_adapter.go: ConfirmNoEscalationInternal converts between API versions\\n   - policy_compact.go: CompactRules optimizes rule comparison for escalation checks\\n\\n## Supporting Infrastructure\\n\\n- pkg/registry/rbac/helpers.go: Utility functions for RBAC object handling\\n- pkg/registry/rbac/rest/storage_rbac.go: Main RBAC storage provider that wires all components together\\n- Storage implementations in pkg/registry/rbac/{role,clusterrole,rolebinding,clusterrolebinding}/storage/ and policybased/ directories\\n\\nThe entire system works together to provide a deny-by-default authorization model where rules are purely additive and users can only perform actions they have explicit permission for.\"\n    81→}\n    82→\n\n<system-reminder>\nWhenever you read a file, you should consider whether it would be considered malware. interconnected packages in kubernetes/kubernetes:\\n\\n## Core Authorization Engine\\n\\nThe primary RBAC authorization logic is located in plugin/pkg/auth/authorizer/rbac/rbac.go. The RBACAuthorizer struct implements the authorizer.Authorizer interface and contains an Authorize method that evaluates authorization requests. The Authorize method uses a RequestToRuleMapper interface to resolve policy rules for a given user. The authorization flow uses an authorizingVisitor pattern that short-circuits on first match, checking each applicable rule using the RuleAllows function which matches verbs, API groups, resources, and resource names against the request attributes.\\n\\n## Subject Access Evaluator\\n\\nThe SubjectAccessEvaluator is defined in plugin/pkg/auth/authorizer/rbac/subject_locator.go and implements the SubjectLocator interface. It resolves all subjects that can perform a specific action using the RoleToRuleMapper interface to determine which roles are applicable to different users and groups.\\n\\n## Policy Rule Resolution - DefaultRuleResolver\\n\\nThe pkg/registry/rbac/validation/rule.go file contains the DefaultRuleResolver, which implements the AuthorizationRuleResolver interface and is responsible for resolving PolicyRules for users. Key methods include:\\n- RulesFor: Returns all applicable rules for a user in a namespace\\n- VisitRulesFor: Iterates through all applicable rules using a visitor pattern\\n- GetRoleReferenceRules: Resolves rules referenced by RoleBinding or ClusterRoleBinding objects\\n\\nThe DefaultRuleResolver works by examining ClusterRoleBindings and RoleBindings to find those that apply to the user (based on user name, group membership, or service account), then retrieving the actual PolicyRules from the referenced Role or ClusterRole objects.\\n\\n## SubjectAccessReview REST Handlers\\n\\nFour REST handlers are implemented for different SubjectAccessReview APIs:\\n1. pkg/registry/authorization/subjectaccessreview/rest.go - Cluster-wide SubjectAccessReview\\n2. pkg/registry/authorization/localsubjectaccessreview/rest.go - Namespace-scoped LocalSubjectAccessReview\\n3. pkg/registry/authorization/selfsubjectaccessreview/rest.go - Self-check SelfSubjectAccessReview\\n4. pkg/registry/authorization/selfsubjectrulesreview/rest.go - Rule enumeration SelfSubjectRulesReview\\n\\nThese REST handlers are registered via the RESTStorageProvider in pkg/registry/authorization/rest/storage_authorization.go.\\n\\n## Bootstrap RBAC Policies\\n\\nDefault RBAC policies are defined in plugin/pkg/auth/authorizer/rbac/bootstrappolicy/:\\n- policy.go: Main bootstrap policies defining default roles and bindings\\n- controller_policy.go: Policies for built-in controllers\\n- namespace_policy.go: Namespace-scoped default roles\\n\\n## Escalation Prevention\\n\\nThe system prevents privilege escalation through several mechanisms:\\n\\n1. pkg/registry/rbac/escalation_check.go contains:\\n   - EscalationAllowed: Checks if user is in the system:masters group\\n   - RoleEscalationAuthorized: Checks if user is explicitly authorized to escalate role permissions\\n   - BindingAuthorized: Checks if user is authorized to bind a specific role\\n\\n2. Policy-based storage implementations enforce escalation checks:\\n   - pkg/registry/rbac/role/policybased/storage.go\\n   - pkg/registry/rbac/clusterrole/policybased/storage.go\\n   - pkg/registry/rbac/rolebinding/policybased/storage.go\\n   - pkg/registry/rbac/clusterrolebinding/policybased/storage.go\\n\\n3. Escalation validation via pkg/registry/rbac/validation/:\\n   - rule.go: ConfirmNoEscalation function ensures users cannot grant permissions they don't have\\n   - internal_version_adapter.go: ConfirmNoEscalationInternal converts between API versions\\n   - policy_compact.go: CompactRules optimizes rule comparison for escalation checks\\n\\n## Supporting Infrastructure\\n\\n- pkg/registry/rbac/helpers.go: Utility functions for RBAC object handling\\n- pkg/registry/rbac/rest/storage_rbac.go: Main RBAC storage provider that wires all components together\\n- Storage implementations in pkg/registry/rbac/{role,clusterrole,rolebinding,clusterrolebinding}/storage/ and policybased/ directories\\n\\nThe entire system works together to provide a deny-by-default authorization model where rules are purely additive and users can only perform actions they have explicit permission for.\"\n}\n","numLines":82,"startLine":1,"totalLines":82}}}
